TFlow introduces weight-space communication: frozen sender agents process the input, and a learned generator maps their hidden states into transient, receiver-specific LoRA perturbations that are fused and applied only during the receiver's generation, enabling per-instance adaptation without permanent weight changes. This approach dramatically reduces token and memory overhead while maintaining collaborative flexibility, offering a more efficient and scalable alternative to message-based agent interactions.","summary_zh":"传统多智能体系统依赖自然语言通信，带来高令牌开销与内存负担。本文提出TFlow框架，将发送者的隐藏状态编译为接收者特定的低秩权重扰动，在生成时动态融合，避免将中间计算序列化为文本。这实现了实例级适应，大幅降低推理成本，为高效且隐私更友好的智能体协作开辟了新路径。","source":"arxiv_cs_cl","title_en":"Good Agentic Friends Do Not Just Give Verbal Advice: They Can Update Your Weights","title_zh":"","theme":"arch","categories_en":["Research"],"categories_zh":["研究"]},{"id":57882462,"url":"http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13838v1","title":"R-DMesh: Video-Guided 3D Animation via Rectified Dynamic Mesh Flow","published_at":"2026-05-13T17:58:13+00:00","original_language":"en","summary_en":"The paper tackles the pose misalignment problem in video-guided 3D animation, where a static mesh’s initial pose rarely matches the video’s start frame, leading to severe distortions. This enables generating high-fidelity 4D animations from arbitrary-pose meshes, making the technique practical for real-world content creation.","summary_zh":"视频引导的3D动画面临初始姿态与视频起始帧不对齐的难题，强行匹配会导致严重变形。为此，该工作提出了R-DMesh框架，通过一种新颖的变分自编码器显式解耦出条件基础网格、相对运动轨迹以及关键的整流跳跃偏移量，从而自动调整输入网格的任意姿态以匹配视频上下文。这一方法实现了高保真4D动画生成，为动画制作提供了更直观、精确的控制手段，具有重要的实践价值。","source":"arxiv_cs_cl","title_en":"R-DMesh: Video-Guided 3D Animation via Rectified Dynamic Mesh Flow","title_zh":"","theme":"arch","categories_en":["Research"],"categories_zh":["研究"]},{"id":4177075016,"url":"http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13833v1","title":"QLAM: A Quantum Long-Attention Memory Approach to Long-Sequence Token Modeling","published_at":"2026-05-13T17:56:20+00:00","original_language":"en","summary_en":"This work tackles the challenge of modeling long-range dependencies in sequential data, where Transformers scale poorly and state-space models (SSMs) often fail to capture complex global token interactions due to their linear, additive updates. The key finding is that the belief in false claims surges dramatically (from 2.5% to 88.6%) after finetuning on such negated documents, and the effect persists unless the negation is embedded within the claim itself rather than in separate sentences.
